                        END;
                      END;

        OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                           CurrReport.PAGENO := 1;
                           GLSetup.GET;
                           IF "Analysis View Name" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                             AnalysisView.GET("Analysis View Name");
                           END ELSE BEGIN
                             AnalysisView.INIT;
                             AnalysisView."Dimension 1 Code" := GLSetup."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                             AnalysisView."Dimension 2 Code" := GLSetup."Global Dimension 2 Code";
                           END;

                           IF UseAmtsInAddCurr THEN
                             HeaderText := STRSUBSTNO(Text003,GLSetup."Additional Reporting Currency")
                           ELSE
                             IF GLSetup."LCY Code" <> '' THEN
                               HeaderText := STRSUBSTNO(Text003,GLSetup."LCY Code")
                             ELSE
                               HeaderText := '';
                         END;

    { PROPERTIES
      {
        DataItemIndent=2;
        DataItemTable=Table85;
        DataItemTableView=SORTING(Schedule Name,Line No.);
        OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                        IF ISSERVICETIER THEN
                          PageGroupNo := NextPageGroupNo;

                        "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Date Filter",DateFilter);
                        "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Budget Filter",BudgetFilter);
                        "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Business Unit Filter",BusinessUnitFilter);
                        "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Dimension 1 Filter",Dim1Filter);
                        "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Dimension 2 Filter",Dim2Filter);
                        "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Dimension 3 Filter",Dim3Filter);
                        "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Dimension 4 Filter",Dim4Filter);
                      END;

        OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                           IF ISSERVICETIER THEN BEGIN
                             CalcColumns;
                             Bold_control := "Acc. Schedule Line".Bold;
                             Italic_control := "Acc. Schedule Line".Italic;
                             Show_control := "Acc. Schedule Line".Show;
                             Underline_control := "Acc. Schedule Line".Underline;
                             ShowOppSign_control := "Acc. Schedule Line"."Show Opposite Sign";
                             NewPage_control := "Acc. Schedule Line"."New Page";
                             NoOfCols_control := NoOfCols;
                             PageGroupNo := NextPageGroupNo;
                             IF "Acc. Schedule Line"."New Page" THEN
                               NextPageGroupNo := PageGroupNo + 1;
                           END
                           ELSE BEGIN
                             FOR i := 1 TO MaxColumnsDisplayed DO BEGIN
                               ColumnValuesDisplayed[i] := 0;
                               ColumnValuesAsText[i] := '';
                             END;

                             IF "Totaling Type" = "Totaling Type"::"Set Base For Percent" THEN
                               CalcColumns;
                           END;
                         END;

        DataItemLinkReference=AccScheduleName;
        DataItemLink=Schedule Name=FIELD(Name);
      }

    PROPERTIES
    {
      Width=6600;
      Height=10450;
      SaveValues=Yes;
      OnOpenForm=BEGIN
                   GLSetup.GET;
                   IF AccSchedNameHidden <> '' THEN
                     AccSchedName := AccSchedNameHidden;
                   IF ColumnLayoutNameHidden <> '' THEN
                     ColumnLayoutName := ColumnLayoutNameHidden;

                   IF AccSchedName <> '' THEN
                     IF NOT AccScheduleName.GET(AccSchedName) THEN
                       AccSchedName := '';
                   IF AccSchedName = '' THEN
                     IF AccScheduleName.FIND('-') THEN
                       AccSchedName := AccScheduleName.Name;

                   IF AccScheduleName."Analysis View Name" <> '' THEN
                     AnalysisView.GET(AccScheduleName."Analysis View Name")
                   ELSE BEGIN
                     AnalysisView."Dimension 1 Code" := GLSetup."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                     AnalysisView."Dimension 2 Code" := GLSetup."Global Dimension 2 Code";
                   END;
                   RequestOptionsForm.Dim1Filter.ENABLED := AnalysisView."Dimension 1 Code" <> '';
                   RequestOptionsForm.Dim2Filter.ENABLED := AnalysisView."Dimension 2 Code" <> '';
                   RequestOptionsForm.Dim3Filter.ENABLED := AnalysisView."Dimension 3 Code" <> '';
                   RequestOptionsForm.Dim4Filter.ENABLED := AnalysisView."Dimension 4 Code" <> '';

                   IF UseHiddenFilters THEN BEGIN
                     DateFilter := DateFilterHidden;
                     BudgetFilter := BudgetFilterHidden;
                     BusinessUnitFilter := BusinessUnitFilterHidden;
                     Dim1Filter := Dim1FilterHidden;
                     Dim2Filter := Dim2FilterHidden;
                     Dim3Filter := Dim3FilterHidden;
                     Dim4Filter := Dim4FilterHidden;
                   END;

                   IF ColumnLayoutName = '' THEN
                     IF AccScheduleName.FIND('-') THEN
                       ColumnLayoutName := AccScheduleName."Default Column Layout";

                   RequestOptionsForm.UPDATECONTROLS;
                 END;

    }

  REQUESTPAGE
  {
    PROPERTIES
    {
      SaveValues=Yes;
      OnInit=BEGIN
               Dim4FilterEnable := TRUE;
               Dim3FilterEnable := TRUE;
               Dim2FilterEnable := TRUE;
               Dim1FilterEnable := TRUE;
             END;

      OnOpenPage=BEGIN
                   GLSetup.GET;
                   IF AccSchedNameHidden <> '' THEN
                     AccSchedName := AccSchedNameHidden;
                   IF ColumnLayoutNameHidden <> '' THEN
                     ColumnLayoutName := ColumnLayoutNameHidden;

                   IF AccSchedName <> '' THEN
                     IF NOT AccScheduleName.GET(AccSchedName) THEN
                       AccSchedName := '';
                   IF AccSchedName = '' THEN
                     IF AccScheduleName.FIND('-') THEN
                       AccSchedName := AccScheduleName.Name;

                   IF AccScheduleName."Analysis View Name" <> '' THEN
                     AnalysisView.GET(AccScheduleName."Analysis View Name")
                   ELSE BEGIN
                     AnalysisView."Dimension 1 Code" := GLSetup."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                     AnalysisView."Dimension 2 Code" := GLSetup."Global Dimension 2 Code";
                   END;
                   Dim1FilterEnable := AnalysisView."Dimension 1 Code" <> '';
                   Dim2FilterEnable := AnalysisView."Dimension 2 Code" <> '';
                   Dim3FilterEnable := AnalysisView."Dimension 3 Code" <> '';
                   Dim4FilterEnable := AnalysisView."Dimension 4 Code" <> '';

                   IF UseHiddenFilters THEN BEGIN
                     DateFilter := DateFilterHidden;
                     BudgetFilter := BudgetFilterHidden;
                     BusinessUnitFilter := BusinessUnitFilterHidden;
                     Dim1Filter := Dim1FilterHidden;
                     Dim2Filter := Dim2FilterHidden;
                     Dim3Filter := Dim3FilterHidden;
                     Dim4Filter := Dim4FilterHidden;
                   END;

                   IF ColumnLayoutName = '' THEN
                     IF AccScheduleName.FIND('-') THEN
                       ColumnLayoutName := AccScheduleName."Default Column Layout";
                 END;

    }
    CONTROLS
    {
      { 1900000001;0;Container;
                  ContainerType=ContentArea }

      { 1900000002;1;Group  ;
                  CaptionML=[ENU=Options;
                             ESP=Opciones] }

      { 28  ;2   ;Group     ;
                  CaptionML=[ENU=Layout;
                             ESP=Disposici¢n] }

      { 3   ;3   ;Field     ;
                  Lookup=Yes;
                  CaptionML=[ENU=Acc. Schedule Name;
                             ESP=Nombre esq. cuentas];
                  SourceExpr=AccSchedName;
                  TableRelation="Acc. Schedule Name";
                  OnValidate=BEGIN
                               AccSchedManagement.CheckName(AccSchedName);
                               AccScheduleName.GET(AccSchedName);
                               IF AccScheduleName."Default Column Layout" <> '' THEN
                                 ColumnLayoutName := AccScheduleName."Default Column Layout";
                               IF AccScheduleName."Analysis View Name" <> '' THEN
                                 AnalysisView.GET(AccScheduleName."Analysis View Name")
                               ELSE BEGIN
                                 CLEAR(AnalysisView);
                                 AnalysisView."Dimension 1 Code" := GLSetup."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                                 AnalysisView."Dimension 2 Code" := GLSetup."Global Dimension 2 Code";
                               END;
                               Dim1FilterEnable := AnalysisView."Dimension 1 Code" <> '';
                               Dim2FilterEnable := AnalysisView."Dimension 2 Code" <> '';
                               Dim3FilterEnable := AnalysisView."Dimension 3 Code" <> '';
                               Dim4FilterEnable := AnalysisView."Dimension 4 Code" <> '';
                             END;

                  OnLookup=BEGIN
                             EXIT(AccSchedManagement.LookupName(AccSchedName,Text));
                           END;
                            }

      { 2   ;3   ;Field     ;
                  Lookup=Yes;
                  CaptionML=[ENU=Column Layout Name;
                             ESP=Nombre plantilla columna];
                  SourceExpr=ColumnLayoutName;

                               IF ColumnLayoutName = '' THEN
                                 ERROR(Text006);

                           END;
                            }

      { 27  ;2   ;Group     ;

                               ApplicationManagement@1001 : Codeunit 1;

  CODE
  {
    VAR
      Text000@1000 : TextConst 'ENU=(Thousands);ESP=(Miles)';
      Text001@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=(Millions);ESP=(Millones)';
      Text002@1002 : TextConst 'ENU=* ERROR *;ESP=* ERROR *';
      Text003@1003 : TextConst 'ENU=All amounts are in %1.;ESP=Todos imp. est n en %1.';
      ColLayoutTmp@1004 : TEMPORARY Record 334;
      AnalysisView@1005 : Record 363;
      GLSetup@1006 : Record 98;
      AccSchedManagement@1007 : Codeunit 8;
      AccSchedName@1028 : Code[10];
      AccSchedNameHidden@1038 : Code[10];
      ColumnLayoutName@1008 : Code[10];
      ColumnLayoutNameHidden@1009 : Code[10];

      DateFilter@1030 : Text[30];
      UseHiddenFilters@1045 : Boolean;

      Dim3FilterHidden@1043 : Text[250];
      Dim4Filter@1036 : Text[250];
      Dim4FilterHidden@1044 : Text[250];
      FiscalStartDate@1013 : Date;
      ColumnValuesDisplayed@1014 : ARRAY [5] OF Decimal;
      ColumnValuesAsText@1015 : ARRAY [5] OF Text[30];
      PeriodText@1016 : Text[30];
      AccSchedLineFilter@1017 : Text[250];
      Header@1018 : ARRAY [5] OF Text[30];
      RoundingHeader@1019 : ARRAY [5] OF Text[30];
      HasRounding@1020 : Boolean;
      i@1021 : Integer;
      MaxColumnsDisplayed@1022 : Integer;
      NoOfCols@1023 : Integer;
      UseAmtsInAddCurr@1024 : Boolean;
      ShowAccSchedSetup@1025 : Boolean;
      HeaderText@1026 : Text[100];

      Text005@1032 : TextConst 'ENU=1,6,,Dimension %1 Filter;ESP=1,6,,Filtro dimensi¢n %1';
      Bold_control@1046 : Boolean;
      Italic_control@1047 : Boolean;
      Show_control@1048 : 'Yes,No,If Any Column Not Zero,When Positive Balance,When Negative Balance';
      Underline_control@1049 : Boolean;
      ShowOppSign_control@1050 : Boolean;
      NewPage_control@1051 : Boolean;
      PageGroupNo@1054 : Integer;
      NextPageGroupNo@1055 : Integer;
      NoOfCols_control@1056 : Integer;

    PROCEDURE InitAccSched@10();
    BEGIN
      AccScheduleName.SETRANGE(Name,AccSchedName);
      "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Date Filter",DateFilter);
      "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Budget Filter",BudgetFilter);
      "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Business Unit Filter",BusinessUnitFilter);
      "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Dimension 1 Filter",Dim1Filter);
      "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Dimension 2 Filter",Dim2Filter);
      "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Dimension 3 Filter",Dim3Filter);
      "Acc. Schedule Line".SETFILTER("Dimension 4 Filter",Dim4Filter);

      StartDate := "Acc. Schedule Line".GETRANGEMIN("Date Filter");
      EndDate := "Acc. Schedule Line".GETRANGEMAX("Date Filter");
      FiscalStartDate := AccSchedManagement.FindFiscalYear(EndDate);

      MaxColumnsDisplayed := ARRAYLEN(ColumnValuesDisplayed);
      AccSchedLineFilter := "Acc. Schedule Line".GETFILTERS;
      PeriodText := "Acc. Schedule Line".GETFILTER("Date Filter");
      HasRounding := FALSE;
      NoOfCols := 0;
      AccSchedManagement.CopyColumnsToTemp(ColumnLayoutName,ColLayoutTmp);
      AccSchedManagement.CheckAnalysisView(AccSchedName,ColumnLayoutName,TRUE);
      WITH ColLayoutTmp DO BEGIN
        i := 0;
        IF FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
          REPEAT
            IF Show <> Show::Never THEN BEGIN
              i := i + 1;
              IF i <= MaxColumnsDisplayed THEN BEGIN
                Header[i] := "Column Header";
                RoundingHeader[i] := '';
                IF "Rounding Factor" IN ["Rounding Factor"::"1000","Rounding Factor"::"1000000"] THEN BEGIN
                  HasRounding := TRUE;
                  CASE "Rounding Factor" OF
                    "Rounding Factor"::"1000":
                      RoundingHeader[i] := Text000;
                    "Rounding Factor"::"1000000":
                      RoundingHeader[i] := Text001;
                  END;
                END;
              END;
            END;
            NoOfCols := NoOfCols + 1;
          UNTIL (i >= MaxColumnsDisplayed) OR (NEXT = 0);
          MaxColumnsDisplayed := i;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetAccSchedName@6(NewAccSchedName@1000 : Code[10]);
    BEGIN
      AccSchedNameHidden := NewAccSchedName;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetColumnLayoutName@1(ColLayoutName@1000 : Code[10]);
    BEGIN
      ColumnLayoutNameHidden := ColLayoutName;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetFilters@4(NewDateFilter@1000 : Text[30];NewBudgetFilter@1001 : Text[30];NewBusUnitFilter@1002 : Text[30];NewDim1Filter@1003 : Text[250];NewDim2Filter@1004 : Text[250];NewDim3Filter@1005 : Text[250];NewDim4Filter@1006 : Text[250]);
    BEGIN
      DateFilterHidden := NewDateFilter;
      BudgetFilterHidden := NewBudgetFilter;
      BusinessUnitFilterHidden := NewBusUnitFilter;
      Dim1FilterHidden := NewDim1Filter;
      Dim2FilterHidden := NewDim2Filter;
      Dim3FilterHidden := NewDim3Filter;
      Dim4FilterHidden := NewDim4Filter;
      UseHiddenFilters := TRUE;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcColumns@2() : Boolean;
    VAR
      NonZero@1000 : Boolean;
      ShowFormulaLine@1001 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      NonZero := FALSE;
      ShowFormulaLine := FALSE;
      WITH ColLayoutTmp DO BEGIN
        SETRANGE("Column Layout Name",ColumnLayoutName);
        i := 0;
        IF FIND('-') THEN
          REPEAT
            IF Show <> Show::Never THEN BEGIN
              i := i + 1;
              ColumnValuesDisplayed[i] :=
                AccSchedManagement.CalcCell("Acc. Schedule Line",ColLayoutTmp,UseAmtsInAddCurr);
              IF AccSchedManagement.GetDivisionError THEN
                IF ShowError IN [ShowError::"Division by Zero",ShowError::Both] THEN
                  ColumnValuesAsText[i] := Text002
                ELSE
                  ColumnValuesAsText[i] := ''
              ELSE IF AccSchedManagement.GetPeriodError THEN
                  IF ShowError IN [ShowError::"Period Error",ShowError::Both] THEN
                    ColumnValuesAsText[i] := Text004
                  ELSE
                    ColumnValuesAsText[i] := ''
              ELSE BEGIN
                  NonZero := NonZero OR (ColumnValuesDisplayed[i] <> 0);
                  IF "Acc. Schedule Line"."Totaling Type" = "Acc. Schedule Line"."Totaling Type"::Formula THEN BEGIN
                    IF (ColumnValuesDisplayed[i] > 0) AND
                       ("Acc. Schedule Line".Show = "Acc. Schedule Line".Show::"When Positive Balance")
                    THEN
                      ShowFormulaLine := TRUE
                    ELSE
                      IF (ColumnValuesDisplayed[i] < 0) AND
                         ("Acc. Schedule Line".Show = "Acc. Schedule Line".Show::"When Negative Balance")
                      THEN
                        ShowFormulaLine := TRUE;
                  END;
                  ColumnValuesAsText[i] :=
                    AccSchedManagement.FormatCellAsText(ColLayoutTmp,ColumnValuesDisplayed[i]);
                END;
            END;
          UNTIL (i >= MaxColumnsDisplayed) OR (NEXT = 0);
      END;
      IF "Acc. Schedule Line"."Totaling Type" = "Acc. Schedule Line"."Totaling Type"::Formula THEN
        EXIT(ShowFormulaLine);
      EXIT(NonZero);
    END;

    PROCEDURE ShowLine@3(Bold@1000 : Boolean;Italic@1001 : Boolean) : Boolean;
    VAR
      NonZero@1002 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF "Acc. Schedule Line"."Totaling Type" = "Acc. Schedule Line"."Totaling Type"::"Set Base For Percent" THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      IF "Acc. Schedule Line".Show = "Acc. Schedule Line".Show::No THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      IF "Acc. Schedule Line".Bold <> Bold THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      IF "Acc. Schedule Line".Italic <> Italic THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      NonZero := CalcColumns;
      IF "Acc. Schedule Line".Show IN
        ["Acc. Schedule Line".Show::"If Any Column Not Zero",
         "Acc. Schedule Line".Show::"When Positive Balance",
         "Acc. Schedule Line".Show::"When Negative Balance"]
      THEN
        EXIT(NonZero);
      EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE FormLookUpDimFilter@57(Dim@1000 : Code[20];VAR Text@1001 : Text[1024]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      DimVal@1002 : Record 349;
      DimValList@1003 : Form 560;
    BEGIN
      IF Dim = '' THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      DimValList.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
      DimVal.SETRANGE("Dimension Code",Dim);
      DimValList.SETTABLEVIEW(DimVal);
      IF DimValList.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
        DimValList.GETRECORD(DimVal);
        Text := DimValList.GetSelectionFilter;
        EXIT(TRUE);
      END;
      EXIT(FALSE)
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE FormGetCaptionClass@12(DimNo@1000 : Integer) : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      CASE DimNo OF
        1:
          BEGIN
            IF AnalysisView."Dimension 1 Code" <> '' THEN
              EXIT('1,6,' + AnalysisView."Dimension 1 Code")
            ELSE
              EXIT(STRSUBSTNO(Text005,DimNo));
          END;
        2:
          BEGIN
            IF AnalysisView."Dimension 2 Code" <> '' THEN
              EXIT('1,6,' + AnalysisView."Dimension 2 Code")
            ELSE
              EXIT(STRSUBSTNO(Text005,DimNo));
          END;
        3:
          BEGIN
            IF AnalysisView."Dimension 3 Code" <> '' THEN
              EXIT('1,6,' + AnalysisView."Dimension 3 Code")
            ELSE
              EXIT(STRSUBSTNO(Text005,DimNo));
          END;
        4:
          BEGIN
            IF AnalysisView."Dimension 4 Code" <> '' THEN
              EXIT('1,6,' + AnalysisView."Dimension 4 Code")
            ELSE
              EXIT(STRSUBSTNO(Text005,DimNo));
          END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE PasaParametros@1100253000(pwAccSchedName@1100253000 : Code[10];pwColumnLayoutName@1100253001 : Code[10];pwDateFilter@1100253002 : Text[30];pwBudgetFilter@1100253003 : Code[10]);
    BEGIN
      // PasaParametros

      AccSchedName     := pwAccSchedName;
      ColumnLayoutName := pwColumnLayoutName;
      DateFilter       := pwDateFilter;
      BudgetFilter     := pwBudgetFilter;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Shared Data1 as Object
Shared Data2 as Object
Shared Data3 as Object

Public Function GetData(Num as Integer, Group as integer) as Object
if Group = 1 then
   Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1),Chr(177))))
End If

if Group = 2 then
   Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data2),Chr(177))))
End If

if Group = 3 then
   Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data3),Chr(177))))
End If

End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData as Object,Group as integer)
  If Group = 1 and NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
      Data1 = NewData
  End If

  If Group = 2 and NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
      Data2 = NewData
  End If

  If Group = 3 and NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
      Data3 = NewData
  End If

End Function</Code>
